        <h2>Storyline</h2>
        
        <div class="inline canwrap">
            <p>
                <span>    As the Avengers and their allies have continued to protect the world from threats too large for any one hero to handle, a new danger has emerged from the cosmic shadows: Thanos. A despot of intergalactic infamy, his goal is to collect all six Infinity Stones, artifacts of unimaginable power, and use them to inflict his twisted will on all of reality. Everything the Avengers have fought for has led up to this moment, the fate of Earth and existence has never been more uncertain.</span>
                <em class="nobr">Written by
<a href="/search/title?plot_author=Marvel%20Studios&view=simple&sort=alpha&ref_=tt_stry_pl"
>Marvel Studios</a></em>            </p>

        <h2>Did You Know?</h2>
    <div id="trivia" class="txt-block">
        <h4>Trivia</h4>
    Although not explicitly stated in the movie, Corvus Glaive and Proxima Midnight of The Black Order are husband and wife.        <a href="trivia?ref_=tt_trv_trv"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>
                <hr />
     <div id="goofs"  class="txt-block">
        <h4>Goofs</h4>
Right before Mantis says the line &quot;kick names, take ass&quot;, her eyes are not almost all black as usually seen.        <a href="trivia?tab=gf&ref_=tt_trv_gf"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>   
                <hr />
    <div id="quotes" class="text-block">
        <h4>Quotes</h4>
[<span class="fine">first lines</span>]
<br /><a href="/name/nm0000110/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"
><span class="character">Asgardian Distress Call</span></a>:
This is the Asgardian refugee vessel Statesman. We are under assault. I repeat, we are under assault. The engines are dead, life support failing. Requesting aid from any vessel within range. We are 22 jump points out of Asgard. Our crew is made up of Asgardian families. We have very few soldiers here. This is not a warcraft. I repeat, this is not a warcraft!
<br />        <a href="trivia?tab=qt&ref_=tt_trv_qu"
class="nobr" >See more</a> &raquo;
    </div>
                <hr />
     <div id="crazyCredits"  class="txt-block">
        <h4>Crazy Credits</h4>
    The closing credits appear over a black background. The film title appears at the end, and crumbles to dust.        <a href="trivia?tab=cz&ref_=tt_trv_cc"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>   
                <hr />
     <div id="alternateVersions"  class="txt-block">
        <h4>Alternate Versions</h4>

    <div class="article" id="titleUserReviewsTeaser">
        <h2>User Reviews</h2>
        <div class="user-comments">
                    <div class="tinystarbar" title="9/10">
                        <div style="width: 90px;">&nbsp;</div>
                    </div>
                <span>
                    <strong>I need a Therapist</strong>
                    <div class="comment-meta">
                        25 April 2018 | by <a href="/user/ur83246523/?ref_=tt_urv"
><span>upashnafuentes</span></a>
                        &ndash; <a href="/user/ur83246523/comments?ref_=tt_urv"
>See all my reviews</a>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                        <p>This movie has made me feel things that I haven&#39;t about a movie in a very long time. If you are anything like me you will definitely feel a sense of &quot;everything is gonna be alright&quot; because of the generous sprinkling of light humour that makes the situation feel less serious than it actually is. The emotional roller coaster that begins right at the beginning of the movie to the very end has you feeling more and more frustrated and on edge as it goes on. Don&#39;t get me wrong this movie is absolutely stunning and amazing and a cliffhanger at the end has you wanting more and more. I&#39;m definitely very excited to see how this storyline will carry out in the next Avengers movie.</p>
                    </div>
                </span>
